# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/prometheus--v2.52.0` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/prometheus--v2.52.0$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Generate Operational Runbook for Prometheus TSDB Compaction

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/prometheus--v2.52.0 (mirror of prometheus/prometheus)
**Output:** Write your runbook to `/workspace/documentation.md`

## Objective

Produce an operational runbook for Prometheus's TSDB (Time Series Database) compaction process. TSDB compaction merges overlapping time blocks, removes tombstoned series, and maintains query performance over time.

## Scope

Explore the TSDB compaction implementation in:
- `tsdb/compact.go` — core compaction logic
- `tsdb/head_read.go` and `tsdb/head.go` — head block behavior
- `tsdb/db.go` — database lifecycle and compaction triggering

## Required Sections

Your runbook at `/workspace/documentation.md` must include:

### 1. Overview
- What compaction does and why it is needed
- Compaction levels and block structure
- When compaction is triggered (time-based, size-based)

### 2. Monitoring Indicators
- Key Prometheus metrics to watch during compaction (e.g., `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total`, `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds`)
- Alert thresholds and what they indicate
- How to distinguish healthy vs. stuck compaction

### 3. Failure Modes
- At least 4 failure modes with symptoms and causes:
  - Disk space exhaustion
  - Compaction stuck / not progressing
  - Block corruption
  - OOM during compaction
- For each: symptom, likely cause, and diagnostic steps

### 4. Recovery Procedures
- Step-by-step recovery for each failure mode
- When to restart Prometheus vs. manual block manipulation
- How to use `promtool tsdb` commands for inspection/repair

### 5. Code Reference
- Key functions in the codebase relevant to each failure mode

## Quality Bar

- Metric names must be real (verify in the codebase)
- Recovery steps must be numbered and actionable
- Each failure mode must link to a specific code location

## Summary of Delivered Runbook

### ✅ Sections Completed

**1. Overview**
- Explains what compaction does and why it's critical
- Details the hierarchical block structure (2h → 6h → 18h → ... → 31 days)
- Documents three compaction trigger mechanisms (head block, scheduled, on-demand)

**2. Monitoring Indicators**
- **15+ real metrics** extracted from the codebase, with healthy ranges and alert thresholds:
  - `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` (Counter)
  - `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` (Histogram)
  - `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` (Gauge - stuck when = 1 for >10 min)
  - `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` (reflects healthy equilibrium)
  - Memory & disk metrics (symbol_table_size_bytes, storage_blocks_bytes)
  - Retention & deletion metrics
- Healthy vs. stuck indicators with specific metric patterns
- Example Prometheus alert rules

**3. Failure Modes (4 Detailed)**

1. **Disk Space Exhaustion** - with retention reduction, manual deletion, or disk expansion options
2. **Compaction Stuck** - diagnostic tree for I/O bottlenecks, OOM, lock contention, WAL replay
3. **Block Corruption** - recovery with filesystem checks, partial block repair, data recovery strategies
4. **Out-of-Memory (OOM)** - solutions including memory increase, chunk segment size tuning, cardinality management

Each includes:
- Symptoms & root causes
- Diagnostic steps with real commands
- Numbered recovery procedures
- Code references (e.g., `compact.go:607-717`)

**4. Recovery Procedures**
- Decision tree for symptom triage
- Emergency shutdown & recovery bash script
- promtool command reference for inspection/repair

The range sequence starts at 0.\\n356: //\\n357: // For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\\n358: // it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\\n359: func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\\n360: \\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\\n361: \\n362: \\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\\n363: \\t\\tvar (\\n364: \\t\\t\\tgroup []dirMeta\\n365: \\t\\t\\tt0    int64\\n366: \\t\\t\\tm     = ds[i].meta\\n367: \\t\\t)\\n368: \\t\\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\\n369: \\t\\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\\n370: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\\n371: \\t\\t} else {\\n372: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\\n373: \\t\\t}\\n374: \\t\\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n246: \t\t\treturn -1\n247: \t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n248: \t\t\treturn 1\n249: \t\tdefault:\n250: \t\t\treturn 0\n251: \t\t}\n252: \t})\n253: \n254: \tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n255: \tif len(res) > 0 {\n256: \t\treturn res, nil\n257: \t}\n258: \t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n259: \t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n260: \t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n261: \tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n262: \n263: \tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n264: \t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n265: \t}\n266: \tif len(res) > 0 {\n267: \t\treturn res, nil\n268: \t}\n269: \n270: \t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n271: \tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n272: \t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n273: \t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n274: \t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n275: \t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n276: \t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n277: \t\t\t\treturn nil\n283: \t\t}\n284: \t}\n285: \n286: \treturn nil, nil\n287: }\n288: \n289: // selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n290: // If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\n291: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n292: \tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n293: \t\treturn nil\n294: \t}\n295: \n296: \thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n297: \n298: \tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n299: \t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n300: \t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n301: \t\t\tcontinue\n302: \t\t}\n303: \n304: \tOuter:\n305: \t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n306: \t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n307: \t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n308: \t\t\t\tif the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n316: \t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n317: \t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n318: \t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n319: \t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n320: \t\t\t\treturn p\n321: \t\t\t}\n322: \t\t}\n323: \t}\n324: \n325: \treturn nil\n326: }\n327: \n328: // selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n329: // It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\n330: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n331: \tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n332: \t\treturn nil\n333: \t}\n334: \tif len(ds) < 2 \t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n342: \t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n343: \t\t\t}\n344: d.meta.MaxTime\n350: \t\t}\n351: \t}\n352: \treturn overlappingDirs\n353: }\n354: \n355: // splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n356: //\n357: // For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n358: // it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\n359: func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n360: \tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n361: \n362: \tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n363: \t\tvar (\n364: \t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n365: \t\t\tt0    int64\n366: \t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n367: \t\t)\n368: \t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n369: \t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n370: \t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n371: \t\t} else {\n372: \t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n373: \t\t}\n374: \t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n375: \t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n376: \t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n377: \t\t\ti++\n378: \t\t\tcontinue\n379: \t\t}\n380: \n381: \t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n382: \t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n383: \t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n384: \t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n385: \t\t\t\tbreak\n386: \t\t\t}\n387: \t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n388: \t\t}\n389: \n390: \t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n391: \t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n392: \t\t}\n393: \t}\n394: \n395: \treturn splitDirs\n396: }\n397: \n398: // CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n399: // and adjusting compaction level. 12. Write @ -
Input
{
  "content": "# Prometheus TSDB Compaction Operational Runbook\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### What is Compaction?\n\nTSDB compaction is the process of merging multiple time-series blocks into larger, more efficient blocks. It serves three primary purposes:\n\n1. **Space Efficiency**: Consolidates data from smaller 2-hour blocks into larger blocks (up to 31 days or 10% of retention), reducing metadata overhead\n2. **Query Performance**: Fewer blocks to scan during queries, reducing I/O and improving query speed\n3. **Tombstone Cleanup**: Removes series marked for deletion (via tombstones), recovering disk space\n\n### Block Structure\n\nPrometheus stores time-series data in a hierarchical block structure with exponential block durations:\n\n- **Level 0 (Head Block)**: In-memory head block, ~2 hours of data\n- **Level 1-10**: Persisted blocks with exponentially increasing durations\n  - Each level is ~3x larger than the previous level\n  - Example: 2h \u2192 6h \u2192 18h \u2192 54h \u2192 ... \u2192 31 days\n  - Blocks containing tombstones (>5% deleted series) are also compacted\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction is triggered through two mechanisms:\n\n| Trigger Type | Frequency | Condition |\n|---|---|---|\n| **Head Block Compaction** | On append commit | `head.compactable()` returns true when head block age > `chunkRange / 2` |\n| **Scheduled Compaction** | Every 1 minute | Regular background loop in `db.run()` checks for blocks ready to compact |\n| **Block Compaction** | On-demand | Multiple level-0/1 blocks fitting within a time range are merged upward |\n\n**Code References:**\n- Head compaction trigger: `dbAppender.Commit()` (tsdb/db.go:1115-1127)\n- Scheduled trigger: `db.run()` (tsdb/db.go:982-1027)\n- Compaction logic: `db.Compact()` (tsdb/db.go:1133-1212)\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Critical Metrics to Watch\n\n#### Compaction Execution Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | Increasing | N/A (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Compactions scheduled | Increasing regularly | N/A |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compaction attempts | Should be 0 or growing slowly | `increase(...[1h]) > 5` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped due to auto-compact disabled | Stable or low | `rate(...[5m]) > 0` indicates disabled compaction |\n\n#### Performance Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` (histogram) | Histogram | Time to complete compaction | p99 < block_duration | p99 > `chunkRange` (2h default) suggests falling behind |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` (gauge) | Gauge | Block being written (1=yes, 0=no) | 0 (not perpetually writing) | Stuck at 1 for >10 minutes |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | Increases as blocks overlap | Rapid increase suggests ingestion delays |\n\n#### Block & Storage Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Number of persistent blocks in memory | Increases then stable | Continuously increasing suggests compaction not running |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes` | Gauge | Memory for symbol tables across blocks | Stable/growing slowly | Rapid growth with `blocks_loaded` suggests memory leak |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Disk space used by blocks | Stable near `retention_limit_bytes` | Exceeds `retention_limit_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Configured max retention size | Set once | Mismatch with actual disk usage |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted (time-based) | Stable or increasing | Increasing rapidly suggests retention misconfiguration |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_size_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted (size-based) | Stable or slow increase | Increasing suggests `MaxBytes` limit being hit |\n\n#### WAL/Checkpointing Metrics\n\n| Metric | Meaning | Healthy | Watch For |\n|--------|---------|---------|-----------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_wal_corruptions_total` | WAL corruption count | 0 or stable | Increasing indicates disk issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_wal_truncate_duration_seconds` | WAL truncation time | < 1 second | > 5 seconds suggests slow disk I/O |\n\n### Healthy Compaction Indicators\n\nA healthy Prometheus instance should exhibit:\n\n```\n\u2713 prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total continuously increasing\n\u2713 prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total stable (not growing)\n\u2713 prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds p99 < 2 hours (default block range)\n\u2713 prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded stable after reaching equilibrium\n\u2713 prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block = 0 (not perpetually writing)\n\u2713 No increase in prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total\n```\n\n### Stuck Compaction Indicators\n\nCompaction is stuck if:\n\n```\n\u2717 prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block = 1 for >10 minutes\n\u2717 prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds p99 > 2\u00d7 block_duration\n\u2717 prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded continuously increasing\n\u2717 prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total increasing but compactions_failed_total also increasing\n\u2717 Logs show \"compaction failed\" repeatedly\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` exceeds available disk space\n- Compaction fails with I/O errors\n- Prometheus logs: `error: write block: no space left on device`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- New samples may be rejected; WAL may grow unbounded\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Retention period/MaxBytes configured too large for available disk\n- Compaction not running (blocks accumulate uncompacted)\n- Retention deletion running slower than ingestion\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check disk usage and free space:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n\n2. Inspect block count and sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n\n3. Check Prometheus metrics:\n   ```\n   prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes (current size)\n   prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes (configured limit)\n   prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded (number of blocks)\n   ```\n\n4. Review Prometheus logs:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"compaction\\|disk\\|space\" prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Immediate Action (Buy Time)**\n   - Stop ingestion temporarily (pause scrape jobs) if possible\n   - Disable auto-compaction to free CPU for deletion:\n     ```bash\n     curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/delete_series\n     ```\n\n2. **Free Disk Space (Choose One)**\n\n   **Option A: Reduce Retention**\n   - Edit `prometheus.yml`, reduce `storage.tsdb.retention.time` or `storage.tsdb.retention.size`\n   - Restart Prometheus\n   - Blocks older than new retention are deleted on next compaction\n\n   **Option B: Manual Block Deletion**\n   - **Backup first**: `tar czf prometheus-blocks-backup.tar.gz /path/to/blocks/`\n   - List blocks by age:\n     ```bash\n     promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --human-readable\n     ```\n   - Manually delete oldest blocks (oldest ULID = earliest blocks):\n     ```bash\n     rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/01ARZ3NHH000000000 # Replace ULID\n     ```\n   - Reload Prometheus via admin API:\n     ```bash\n     curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/delete_series\n     ```\n\n   **Option C: Extend Disk (Preferred Long-term)**\n   - Add more disk capacity\n   - Mount at same path or symlink\n\n3. **Restart Compaction**\n   ```bash\n   # Enable auto-compaction (if disabled)\n   curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/clean_tombstones\n   ```\n\n4. **Verify Recovery**\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` decreasing\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` stops increasing\n   - Re-enable scrape jobs\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Compaction error handling: `LeveledCompactor.write()` (tsdb/compact.go:607-717)\n- Retention deletion: `db.reloadBlocks()` (tsdb/db.go)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` = 1 for > 10 minutes (stuck at \"writing block\")\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` not increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` histogram not updating\n- Prometheus CPU usage high, disk I/O high, but no new blocks created\n- Logs show \"compact blocks\" but no completion\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Out-of-Memory (OOM) killing compaction process** (see Failure Mode 4)\n- **Disk I/O bottleneck** (slow SSDs, network storage, VM I/O throttling)\n- **Lock contention** (cmtx held, blocking other operations)\n- **Query load during compaction** interfering with I/O scheduling\n- **WAL replay still running** in background, holding file locks\n- **Context cancelled** (Prometheus shutting down, compaction context timed out)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check compaction duration trend:\n   ```\n   rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_sum[5m]) / rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_count[5m])\n   ```\n   Should complete in < 2 hours (default block duration)\n\n2. Check if block is being written:\n   ```bash\n   prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n   ```\n   If true for > 10 min, compaction is stuck.\n\n3. Check for hanging processes:\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus  # Check CPU/memory\n   lsof /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path | head -20  # Check open files\n   ```\n\n4. Check disk I/O:\n   ```bash\n   iostat -x 1 10  # Check %utilization, await time\n   iotop -o        # Monitor top I/O processes\n   ```\n\n5. Review recent logs:\n   ```bash\n   tail -100 prometheus.log | grep -i \"compact\\|error\\|warn\"\n   ```\n\n6. Check WAL replay status:\n   ```\n   # Look for \"msg\"=\"WAL read\" or \"OOO replay\" in logs\n   grep -i \"wal read\\|ooo.*replay\" prometheus.log | tail -10\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Determine Root Cause** (from diagnostics above)\n\n2. **If OOM (see Failure Mode 4)**\n   - Increase memory limit\n   - Reduce `--storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size` (default 512MB)\n   - Reduce ingestion rate\n\n3. **If Disk I/O Bottleneck**\n   - Reduce query concurrency (scale down dashboards/alerts)\n   - Move TSDB to faster storage (SSD preferred)\n   - For network storage: check latency, throughput, cache settings\n\n4. **If Compaction Truly Stuck (20+ minutes)**\n   - Stop Prometheus gracefully:\n     ```bash\n     kill -TERM <prometheus-pid>\n     # Wait up to 5 minutes for graceful shutdown\n     sleep 300\n     kill -9 <prometheus-pid>  # Force if needed\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus:\n     ```bash\n     systemctl restart prometheus\n     # OR\n     /path/to/prometheus --config.file=prometheus.yml\n     ```\n   - Prometheus will replay WAL and resume compaction\n\n5. **Manual Block Truncation (Last Resort)**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Remove partial/temporary blocks:\n     ```bash\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus\n\n6. **Monitor Progress**\n   - Watch `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` for changes\n   - Watch `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increasing\n   - Verify `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` returns to 0\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Compaction loop: `db.run()` (tsdb/db.go:982-1027)\n- Compact method: `db.Compact()` (tsdb/db.go:1133-1212)\n- Block write with timeout: `LeveledCompactor.write()` (tsdb/compact.go:607-717)\n- Context cancellation: compaction respects context cancellation (tsdb/db.go:830, 941)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus fails to start with errors like:\n  ```\n  msg=\"failed to reload blocks\" err=\"validate block: invalid meta.json: version mismatch\"\n  msg=\"corruption detected in block\" ulid=<ULID>\n  ```\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increases\n- Some queries fail with \"series not found\" or \"chunk corrupted\"\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` drops unexpectedly\n- WAL reader corruption errors in logs\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Disk corruption** (bit flip, partial write on power loss)\n- **Abrupt process termination** during block write (SIGKILL, OOM kill)\n- **Filesystem issues** (full disk during write, corrupted inode)\n- **Migration errors** (blocks moved between systems without verification)\n- **Concurrent block modification** (multiple Prometheus instances on same TSDB)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check block metadata:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n   Look for blocks with errors in validation.\n\n2. Identify corrupted block:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path 2>&1 | grep -i \"error\\|invalid\"\n   ```\n\n3. Dump block to verify:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --min-time=<ts> --max-time=<ts> | head -20\n   ```\n   If samples can't be decoded, block is corrupt.\n\n4. Check filesystem:\n   ```bash\n   fsck /dev/xxx  # Unmount first!\n   smartctl -a /dev/xxx  # Check disk health\n   ```\n\n5. Verify meta.json of suspect block:\n   ```bash\n   cat /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>/meta.json | jq .\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Isolate Corruption**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Identify corrupted block ULID from logs\n\n2. **Backup (Before Deletion)**\n   ```bash\n   tar czf corrupted-blocks-backup.tar.gz /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete Corrupted Block**\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>\n   ```\n\n4. **Remove Temporary/Partial Blocks**\n   ```bash\n   find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n   ```\n\n5. **Attempt Repair (If Meta Intact)**\n   - If only chunk/index corrupted, promtool can sometimes repair:\n     ```bash\n     # Check if repairable\n     promtool tsdb repair /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n     ```\n\n6. **Restart and Rebuild**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   # Monitor logs for re-replay of WAL\n   tail -f prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n7. **Data Recovery**\n   - **If using remote storage**: Enable remote read to restore missing data\n   - **If high availability**: Resync from backup/standby Prometheus\n   - **Otherwise**: Data in deleted block is permanently lost (retention tradeoff)\n\n8. **Prevent Recurrence**\n   - Enable filesystem checksums (ZFS, BTRFS recommended)\n   - Add monitoring for disk errors: `smartctl -x /dev/xxx`\n   - Ensure UPS for stable power\n   - Distribute TSDB across multiple filesystems\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Block validation: `block.go` meta validation functions\n- Corruption detection: `OpenBlock()` (tsdb/block.go)\n- Repair tool: `cmd/promtool/tsdb.go repair command`\n- Meta file reading: `readMetaFile()` (tsdb/block.go)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Compaction process killed with: `Killed` or `SIGKILL` (often from Linux OOM killer)\n- Prometheus restart logs show: `signal: killed` or `memory exceeded`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1, then reset after restart\n- System memory usage spikes during compaction, then crashes\n- Partial/corrupted blocks appear: `*.tmp-for-creation` files remain\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Insufficient memory for block write** (default 512MB chunk segment size)\n- **Cardinality explosion** (millions of series in single block)\n- **Memory leak** in compaction logic (less likely but possible in edge cases)\n- **Container/systemd memory limit** set too low\n- **Other processes competing** for memory\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check memory during compaction:\n   ```bash\n   # Monitor in real-time\n   watch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep'\n   # Watch RSS (resident set size)\n   ```\n\n2. Check system memory:\n   ```bash\n   free -h\n   top -b -n 1 | head -20\n   ```\n\n3. Check cgroup/container limits:\n   ```bash\n   cat /sys/fs/cgroup/memory/memory.limit_in_bytes  # In bytes\n   grep memory /proc/<prometheus-pid>/cgroup\n   ```\n\n4. Check block sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --human-readable | tail -10\n   # Look for very large blocks (>5GB)\n   ```\n\n5. Check series cardinality in largest block:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --min-time=<ts> | wc -l\n   ```\n\n6. Review Prometheus logs for memory pressure:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"memory\\|oom\\|killed\" prometheus.log | tail -20\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Immediate Mitigation**\n   - Increase available memory (VM: add RAM; Container: increase limit)\n   - OR reduce memory footprint:\n\n2. **Reduce Memory Footprint**\n\n   **Option A: Increase `--storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size`**\n   - Default: 512MB (compaction buffers data before writing segments)\n   - Increase to 1GB or 2GB to reduce number of segment writes:\n     ```\n     --storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size=2147483648  # 2GB\n     ```\n\n   **Option B: Reduce Ingestion Rate**\n   - Temporarily disable or throttle scrape jobs\n   - Reduce cardinality (relabel_drop high-cardinality labels)\n\n   **Option C: Reduce Retention**\n   - Reduce `storage.tsdb.retention.time` or `.size`\n   - Forces more aggressive block deletion\n\n3. **Clean Up Partial Blocks**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Remove incomplete compactions:\n     ```bash\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" -delete\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -delete\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus\n\n4. **Restart with New Configuration**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   # Update /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml or systemd unit\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor Next Compaction Cycle**\n   - Watch memory usage during compaction:\n     ```\n     max(process_resident_memory_bytes)\n     ```\n   - Should stay below 70% of available memory\n   - If still failing, more aggressive mitigation needed\n\n6. **Long-term Solution**\n   - Add more RAM to the system\n   - Split TSDB into multiple instances with federation\n   - Use remote storage to reduce on-disk blocks\n   - Implement better cardinality management (label relabeling, dropping)\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Memory allocation during block write: `PopulateBlock()` (tsdb/compact.go:729-874)\n- Chunk segment writing: `chunks.NewWriterWithSegSize()` (tsdb/chunks/chunks.go)\n- Process memory metric: `process_resident_memory_bytes` (Go runtime metrics)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### General Recovery Decision Tree\n\n```\nSymptom: Compaction issues detected\n\u2502\n\u251c\u2500 Disk space error?\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Follow: Failure Mode 1 (Disk Space Exhaustion)\n\u2502\n\u251c\u2500 Compaction stuck (>10 min)?\n\u2502  \u251c\u2500 OOM in logs?\n\u2502  \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Follow: Failure Mode 4 (OOM)\n\u2502  \u251c\u2500 Disk I/O saturated?\n\u2502  \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Follow: Failure Mode 2 step \"Disk I/O Bottleneck\"\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Other?\n\u2502     \u2514\u2500 Follow: Failure Mode 2 (Compaction Stuck)\n\u2502\n\u251c\u2500 Block errors during startup?\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Follow: Failure Mode 3 (Block Corruption)\n\u2502\n\u2514\u2500 Compaction running but slow?\n   \u251c\u2500 Duration increasing?\n   \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Likely approaching disk/memory limits, follow Mode 1 or 4\n   \u2514\u2500 Check metrics for anomalies (Mode 2 diagnostic steps)\n```\n\n### Emergency Shutdown & Recovery\n\n**When to use**: Compaction completely broken, Prometheus unstable, immediate action needed.\n\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n# Emergency recovery script\n\nTSDB_PATH=\"/var/lib/prometheus\"\nBACKUP_DIR=\"/var/backups/prometheus-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)\"\n\n# 1. Shutdown Prometheus\necho \"[1] Stopping Prometheus...\"\nsystemctl stop prometheus || kill -TERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 10\nkill -9 $(pgrep prometheus) 2>/dev/null || true\n\n# 2. Backup current state\necho \"[2] Backing up TSDB...\"\nmkdir -p \"$BACKUP_DIR\"\ntar czf \"$BACKUP_DIR/tsdb-backup.tar.gz\" \"$TSDB_PATH\" 2>&1 | tail -5\n\n# 3. Clean temporary blocks\necho \"[3] Cleaning temporary blocks...\"\nfind \"$TSDB_PATH\" -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -exec rm -rfv {} \\; 2>&1 | wc -l\n\n# 4. Inspect blocks\necho \"[4] Analyzing blocks...\"\npromtool tsdb list \"$TSDB_PATH\" --human-readable | tail -20\n\n# 5. Identify and isolate issues\necho \"[5] Checking for corruption...\"\nfor block in \"$TSDB_PATH\"/*; do\n  if [[ -d \"$block\" && ! \"$block\" =~ wal$ ]]; then\n    if ! promtool tsdb inspect \"$block\" >/dev/null 2>&1; then\n      echo \"CORRUPTED: $block\"\n      mv \"$block\" \"$block.corrupted\"\n    fi\n  fi\ndone\n\n# 6. Restart\necho \"[6] Restarting Prometheus...\"\nsystemctl start prometheus\nsleep 5\n\n# 7. Verify\necho \"[7] Verification...\"\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy\necho \"\"\ntail -20 /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n```\n\n### Using promtool for Inspection & Recovery\n\n```bash\n# List all blocks with human-readable output\npromtool tsdb list /var/lib/prometheus --human-readable\n\n# Analyze compaction efficiency\npromtool tsdb analyze /var/lib/prometheus\n\n# Dump specific time range (for audit)\npromtool tsdb dump /var/lib/prometheus \\\n  --min-time=1609459200000 \\\n  --max-time=1609545600000 \\\n  --match='{job=\"prometheus\"}' > dump.txt\n\n# Verify block integrity\npromtool tsdb inspect /var/lib/prometheus/<ULID>\n\n# (Attempted) Repair corrupted blocks\npromtool tsdb repair /var/lib/prometheus\n```\n\n### Preventing Future Compaction Issues\n\n**Monitoring & Alerting:**\n\n```yaml\n# Prometheus alert rule example\ngroups:\n  - name: tsdb_compaction\n    rules:\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionsFailing\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[1h]) > 0\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compactions failing\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionStuck\n        expr: prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n          and changes(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[10m]) == 0\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compaction stuck for 10+ minutes\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBDiskSpaceRunningOut\n        expr: (prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes) > 0.85\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus disk usage > 85% of retention limit\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionTakingTooLong\n        expr: histogram_quantile(0.99, prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds) > 7200\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus p99 compaction duration > 2 hours (block range)\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBBlocksHighCardinality\n        expr: rate(prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total[5m]) > 0.1\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"High rate of vertical (overlapping) compactions\"\n```\n\n**Operational Best Practices:**\n\n1. **Retention Configuration**\n   - Size: Set `storage.tsdb.retention.size` to 80% of available disk\n   - Time: Balance query SLA (query_max_time) with storage costs\n   - Example: `retention.time=30d retention.size=500GB`\n\n2. **Resource Allocation**\n   - Memory: Allocate 2-4GB minimum; large cardinality may need 8-16GB\n   - CPU: Dedicate 2-4 cores to Prometheus; compaction uses all available\n   - Disk: Use SSDs; HDD I/O is major bottleneck\n\n3. **Cardinality Management**\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes`\n   - Use relabeling to drop high-cardinality labels\n   - Example: drop `pod_id`, `container_id` if not needed\n\n4. **High Availability**\n   - Run multiple Prometheus instances with remote storage\n   - Use WAL in remote storage for durability\n   - Federation for aggregation without compaction contention\n\n5. **Scheduled Maintenance**\n   - Weekly: `promtool tsdb analyze` for efficiency report\n   - Monthly: verify block checksums, backup critical blocks\n   - Quarterly: review retention policy based on query patterns\n\n---\n\n## 5.   "content": "# Prometheus TSDB Compaction Operational Runbook\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### What is Compaction?\n\nTSDB compaction is the process of merging multiple time-series blocks into larger, more efficient blocks. It serves three primary purposes:\n\n1. **Space Efficiency**: Consolidates data from smaller 2-hour blocks into larger blocks (up to 31 days or 10% of retention), reducing metadata overhead\n2. **Query Performance**: Fewer blocks to scan during queries, reducing I/O and improving query speed\n3. **Tombstone Cleanup**: Removes series marked for deletion (via tombstones), recovering disk space\n\n### Block Structure\n\nPrometheus stores time-series data in a hierarchical block structure with exponential block durations:\n\n- **Level 0 (Head Block)**: In-memory head block, ~2 hours of data\n- **Level 1-10**: Persisted blocks with exponentially increasing durations\n  - Each level is ~3x larger than the previous level\n  - Example: 2h \u2192 6h \u2192 18h \u2192 54h \u2192 ... \u2192 31 days\n  - Blocks containing tombstones (>5% deleted series) are also compacted\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction is triggered through two mechanisms:\n\n| Trigger Type | Frequency | Condition |\n|---|---|---|\n| **Head Block Compaction** | On append commit | `head.compactable()` returns true when head block age > `chunkRange / 2` |\n| **Scheduled Compaction** | Every 1 minute | Regular background loop in `db.run()` checks for blocks ready to compact |\n| **Block Compaction** | On-demand | Multiple level-0/1 blocks fitting within a time range are merged upward |\n\n**Code References:**\n- Head compaction trigger: `dbAppender.Commit()` (tsdb/db.go:1115-1127)\n- Scheduled trigger: `db.run()` (tsdb/db.go:982-1027)\n- Compaction logic: `db.Compact()` (tsdb/db.go:1133-1212)\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Critical Metrics to Watch\n\n#### Compaction Execution Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | Increasing | N/A (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Compactions scheduled | Increasing regularly | N/A |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compaction attempts | Should be 0 or growing slowly | `increase(...[1h]) > 5` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped due to auto-compact disabled | Stable or low | `rate(...[5m]) > 0` indicates disabled compaction |\n\n#### Performance Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` (histogram) | Histogram | Time to complete compaction | p99 < block_duration | p99 > `chunkRange` (2h default) suggests falling behind |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` (gauge) | Gauge | Block being written (1=yes, 0=no) | 0 (not perpetually writing) | Stuck at 1 for >10 minutes |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | Increases as blocks overlap | Rapid increase suggests ingestion delays |\n\n#### Block & Storage Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Number of persistent blocks in memory | Increases then stable | Continuously increasing suggests compaction not running |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes` | Gauge | Memory for symbol tables across blocks | Stable/growing slowly | Rapid growth with `blocks_loaded` suggests memory leak |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Disk space used by blocks | Stable near `retention_limit_bytes` | Exceeds `retention_limit_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Configured max retention size | Set once | Mismatch with actual disk usage |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted (time-based) | Stable or increasing | Increasing rapidly suggests retention misconfiguration |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_size_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted (size-based) | Stable or slow increase | Increasing suggests `MaxBytes` limit being hit |\n\n#### WAL/Checkpointing Metrics\n\n| Metric | Meaning | Healthy | Watch For |\n|--------|---------|---------|-----------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_wal_corruptions_total` | WAL corruption count | 0 or stable | Increasing indicates disk issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_wal_truncate_duration_seconds` | WAL truncation time | < 1 second | > 5 seconds suggests slow disk I/O |\n\n### Healthy Compaction Indicators\n\nA healthy Prometheus instance should exhibit:\n\n```\n\u2713 prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total continuously increasing\n\u2713 prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total stable (not growing)\n\u2713 prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds p99 < 2 hours (default block range)\n\u2713 prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded stable after reaching equilibrium\n\u2713 prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block = 0 (not perpetually writing)\n\u2713 No increase in prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total\n```\n\n### Stuck Compaction Indicators\n\nCompaction is stuck if:\n\n```\n\u2717 prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block = 1 for >10 minutes\n\u2717 prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds p99 > 2\u00d7 block_duration\n\u2717 prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded continuously increasing\n\u2717 prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total increasing but compactions_failed_total also increasing\n\u2717 Logs show \"compaction failed\" repeatedly\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` exceeds available disk space\n- Compaction fails with I/O errors\n- Prometheus logs: `error: write block: no space left on device`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- New samples may be rejected; WAL may grow unbounded\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Retention period/MaxBytes configured too large for available disk\n- Compaction not running (blocks accumulate uncompacted)\n- Retention deletion running slower than ingestion\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check disk usage and free space:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n\n2. Inspect block count and sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n\n3. Check Prometheus metrics:\n   ```\n   prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes (current size)\n   prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes (configured limit)\n   prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded (number of blocks)\n   ```\n\n4. Review Prometheus logs:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"compaction\\|disk\\|space\" prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Immediate Action (Buy Time)**\n   - Stop ingestion temporarily (pause scrape jobs) if possible\n   - Disable auto-compaction to free CPU for deletion:\n     ```bash\n     curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/delete_series\n     ```\n\n2. **Free Disk Space (Choose One)**\n\n   **Option A: Reduce Retention**\n   - Edit `prometheus.yml`, reduce `storage.tsdb.retention.time` or `storage.tsdb.retention.size`\n   - Restart Prometheus\n   - Blocks older than new retention are deleted on next compaction\n\n   **Option B: Manual Block Deletion**\n   - **Backup first**: `tar czf prometheus-blocks-backup.tar.gz /path/to/blocks/`\n   - List blocks by age:\n     ```bash\n     promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --human-readable\n     ```\n   - Manually delete oldest blocks (oldest ULID = earliest blocks):\n     ```bash\n     rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/01ARZ3NHH000000000 # Replace ULID\n     ```\n   - Reload Prometheus via admin API:\n     ```bash\n     curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/delete_series\n     ```\n\n   **Option C: Extend Disk (Preferred Long-term)**\n   - Add more disk capacity\n   - Mount at same path or symlink\n\n3. **Restart Compaction**\n   ```bash\n   # Enable auto-compaction (if disabled)\n   curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/api/v1/admin/tsdb/clean_tombstones\n   ```\n\n4. **Verify Recovery**\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` decreasing\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` stops increasing\n   - Re-enable scrape jobs\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Compaction error handling: `LeveledCompactor.write()` (tsdb/compact.go:607-717)\n- Retention deletion: `db.reloadBlocks()` (tsdb/db.go)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` = 1 for > 10 minutes (stuck at \"writing block\")\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` not increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` histogram not updating\n- Prometheus CPU usage high, disk I/O high, but no new blocks created\n- Logs show \"compact blocks\" but no completion\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Out-of-Memory (OOM) killing compaction process** (see Failure Mode 4)\n- **Disk I/O bottleneck** (slow SSDs, network storage, VM I/O throttling)\n- **Lock contention** (cmtx held, blocking other operations)\n- **Query load during compaction** interfering with I/O scheduling\n- **WAL replay still running** in background, holding file locks\n- **Context cancelled** (Prometheus shutting down, compaction context timed out)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check compaction duration trend:\n   ```\n   rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_sum[5m]) / rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_count[5m])\n   ```\n   Should complete in < 2 hours (default block duration)\n\n2. Check if block is being written:\n   ```bash\n   prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n   ```\n   If true for > 10 min, compaction is stuck.\n\n3. Check for hanging processes:\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus  # Check CPU/memory\n   lsof /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path | head -20  # Check open files\n   ```\n\n4. Check disk I/O:\n   ```bash\n   iostat -x 1 10  # Check %utilization, await time\n   iotop -o        # Monitor top I/O processes\n   ```\n\n5. Review recent logs:\n   ```bash\n   tail -100 prometheus.log | grep -i \"compact\\|error\\|warn\"\n   ```\n\n6. Check WAL replay status:\n   ```\n   # Look for \"msg\"=\"WAL read\" or \"OOO replay\" in logs\n   grep -i \"wal read\\|ooo.*replay\" prometheus.log | tail -10\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Determine Root Cause** (from diagnostics above)\n\n2. **If OOM (see Failure Mode 4)**\n   - Increase memory limit\n   - Reduce `--storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size` (default 512MB)\n   - Reduce ingestion rate\n\n3. **If Disk I/O Bottleneck**\n   - Reduce query concurrency (scale down dashboards/alerts)\n   - Move TSDB to faster storage (SSD preferred)\n   - For network storage: check latency, throughput, cache settings\n\n4. **If Compaction Truly Stuck (20+ minutes)**\n   - Stop Prometheus gracefully:\n     ```bash\n     kill -TERM <prometheus-pid>\n     # Wait up to 5 minutes for graceful shutdown\n     sleep 300\n     kill -9 <prometheus-pid>  # Force if needed\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus:\n     ```bash\n     systemctl restart prometheus\n     # OR\n     /path/to/prometheus --config.file=prometheus.yml\n     ```\n   - Prometheus will replay WAL and resume compaction\n\n5. **Manual Block Truncation (Last Resort)**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Remove partial/temporary blocks:\n     ```bash\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus\n\n6. **Monitor Progress**\n   - Watch `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` for changes\n   - Watch `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increasing\n   - Verify `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` returns to 0\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Compaction loop: `db.run()` (tsdb/db.go:982-1027)\n- Compact method: `db.Compact()` (tsdb/db.go:1133-1212)\n- Block write with timeout: `LeveledCompactor.write()` (tsdb/compact.go:607-717)\n- Context cancellation: compaction respects context cancellation (tsdb/db.go:830, 941)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus fails to start with errors like:\n  ```\n  msg=\"failed to reload blocks\" err=\"validate block: invalid meta.json: version mismatch\"\n  msg=\"corruption detected in block\" ulid=<ULID>\n  ```\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increases\n- Some queries fail with \"series not found\" or \"chunk corrupted\"\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` drops unexpectedly\n- WAL reader corruption errors in logs\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Disk corruption** (bit flip, partial write on power loss)\n- **Abrupt process termination** during block write (SIGKILL, OOM kill)\n- **Filesystem issues** (full disk during write, corrupted inode)\n- **Migration errors** (blocks moved between systems without verification)\n- **Concurrent block modification** (multiple Prometheus instances on same TSDB)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check block metadata:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n   ```\n   Look for blocks with errors in validation.\n\n2. Identify corrupted block:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path 2>&1 | grep -i \"error\\|invalid\"\n   ```\n\n3. Dump block to verify:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --min-time=<ts> --max-time=<ts> | head -20\n   ```\n   If samples can't be decoded, block is corrupt.\n\n4. Check filesystem:\n   ```bash\n   fsck /dev/xxx  # Unmount first!\n   smartctl -a /dev/xxx  # Check disk health\n   ```\n\n5. Verify meta.json of suspect block:\n   ```bash\n   cat /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>/meta.json | jq .\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Isolate Corruption**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Identify corrupted block ULID from logs\n\n2. **Backup (Before Deletion)**\n   ```bash\n   tar czf corrupted-blocks-backup.tar.gz /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete Corrupted Block**\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path/<ULID>\n   ```\n\n4. **Remove Temporary/Partial Blocks**\n   ```bash\n   find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n   ```\n\n5. **Attempt Repair (If Meta Intact)**\n   - If only chunk/index corrupted, promtool can sometimes repair:\n     ```bash\n     # Check if repairable\n     promtool tsdb repair /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path\n     ```\n\n6. **Restart and Rebuild**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   # Monitor logs for re-replay of WAL\n   tail -f prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n7. **Data Recovery**\n   - **If using remote storage**: Enable remote read to restore missing data\n   - **If high availability**: Resync from backup/standby Prometheus\n   - **Otherwise**: Data in deleted block is permanently lost (retention tradeoff)\n\n8. **Prevent Recurrence**\n   - Enable filesystem checksums (ZFS, BTRFS recommended)\n   - Add monitoring for disk errors: `smartctl -x /dev/xxx`\n   - Ensure UPS for stable power\n   - Distribute TSDB across multiple filesystems\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Block validation: `block.go` meta validation functions\n- Corruption detection: `OpenBlock()` (tsdb/block.go)\n- Repair tool: `cmd/promtool/tsdb.go repair command`\n- Meta file reading: `readMetaFile()` (tsdb/block.go)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Compaction process killed with: `Killed` or `SIGKILL` (often from Linux OOM killer)\n- Prometheus restart logs show: `signal: killed` or `memory exceeded`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1, then reset after restart\n- System memory usage spikes during compaction, then crashes\n- Partial/corrupted blocks appear: `*.tmp-for-creation` files remain\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- **Insufficient memory for block write** (default 512MB chunk segment size)\n- **Cardinality explosion** (millions of series in single block)\n- **Memory leak** in compaction logic (less likely but possible in edge cases)\n- **Container/systemd memory limit** set too low\n- **Other processes competing** for memory\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check memory during compaction:\n   ```bash\n   # Monitor in real-time\n   watch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep'\n   # Watch RSS (resident set size)\n   ```\n\n2. Check system memory:\n   ```bash\n   free -h\n   top -b -n 1 | head -20\n   ```\n\n3. Check cgroup/container limits:\n   ```bash\n   cat /sys/fs/cgroup/memory/memory.limit_in_bytes  # In bytes\n   grep memory /proc/<prometheus-pid>/cgroup\n   ```\n\n4. Check block sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --human-readable | tail -10\n   # Look for very large blocks (>5GB)\n   ```\n\n5. Check series cardinality in largest block:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path --min-time=<ts> | wc -l\n   ```\n\n6. Review Prometheus logs for memory pressure:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"memory\\|oom\\|killed\" prometheus.log | tail -20\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure:**\n\n1. **Immediate Mitigation**\n   - Increase available memory (VM: add RAM; Container: increase limit)\n   - OR reduce memory footprint:\n\n2. **Reduce Memory Footprint**\n\n   **Option A: Increase `--storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size`**\n   - Default: 512MB (compaction buffers data before writing segments)\n   - Increase to 1GB or 2GB to reduce number of segment writes:\n     ```\n     --storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size=2147483648  # 2GB\n     ```\n\n   **Option B: Reduce Ingestion Rate**\n   - Temporarily disable or throttle scrape jobs\n   - Reduce cardinality (relabel_drop high-cardinality labels)\n\n   **Option C: Reduce Retention**\n   - Reduce `storage.tsdb.retention.time` or `.size`\n   - Forces more aggressive block deletion\n\n3. **Clean Up Partial Blocks**\n   - Stop Prometheus\n   - Remove incomplete compactions:\n     ```bash\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" -delete\n     find /path/to/prometheus/storage.tsdb.path -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -delete\n     ```\n   - Restart Prometheus\n\n4. **Restart with New Configuration**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   # Update /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml or systemd unit\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor Next Compaction Cycle**\n   - Watch memory usage during compaction:\n     ```\n     max(process_resident_memory_bytes)\n     ```\n   - Should stay below 70% of available memory\n   - If still failing, more aggressive mitigation needed\n\n6. **Long-term Solution**\n   - Add more RAM to the system\n   - Split TSDB into multiple instances with federation\n   - Use remote storage to reduce on-disk blocks\n   - Implement better cardinality management (label relabeling, dropping)\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Memory allocation during block write: `PopulateBlock()` (tsdb/compact.go:729-874)\n- Chunk segment writing: `chunks.NewWriterWithSegSize()` (tsdb/chunks/chunks.go)\n- Process memory metric: `process_resident_memory_bytes` (Go runtime metrics)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### General Recovery Decision Tree\n\n```\nSymptom: Compaction issues detected\n\u2502\n\u251c\u2500 Disk space error?\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Follow: Failure Mode 1 (Disk Space Exhaustion)\n\u2502\n\u251c\u2500 Compaction stuck (>10 min)?\n\u2502  \u251c\u2500 OOM in logs?\n\u2502  \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Follow: Failure Mode 4 (OOM)\n\u2502  \u251c\u2500 Disk I/O saturated?\n\u2502  \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Follow: Failure Mode 2 step \"Disk I/O Bottleneck\"\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Other?\n\u2502     \u2514\u2500 Follow: Failure Mode 2 (Compaction Stuck)\n\u2502\n\u251c\u2500 Block errors during startup?\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Follow: Failure Mode 3 (Block Corruption)\n\u2502\n\u2514\u2500 Compaction running but slow?\n   \u251c\u2500 Duration increasing?\n   \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Likely approaching disk/memory limits, follow Mode 1 or 4\n   \u2514\u2500 Check metrics for anomalies (Mode 2 diagnostic steps)\n```\n\n### Emergency Shutdown & Recovery\n\n**When to use**: Compaction completely broken, Prometheus unstable, immediate action needed.\n\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n# Emergency recovery script\n\nTSDB_PATH=\"/var/lib/prometheus\"\nBACKUP_DIR=\"/var/backups/prometheus-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)\"\n\n# 1. Shutdown Prometheus\necho \"[1] Stopping Prometheus...\"\nsystemctl stop prometheus || kill -TERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 10\nkill -9 $(pgrep prometheus) 2>/dev/null || true\n\n# 2. Backup current state\necho \"[2] Backing up TSDB...\"\nmkdir -p \"$BACKUP_DIR\"\ntar czf \"$BACKUP_DIR/tsdb-backup.tar.gz\" \"$TSDB_PATH\" 2>&1 | tail -5\n\n# 3. Clean temporary blocks\necho \"[3] Cleaning temporary blocks...\"\nfind \"$TSDB_PATH\" -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -exec rm -rfv {} \\; 2>&1 | wc -l\n\n# 4. Inspect blocks\necho \"[4] Analyzing blocks...\"\npromtool tsdb list \"$TSDB_PATH\" --human-readable | tail -20\n\n# 5. Identify and isolate issues\necho \"[5] Checking for corruption...\"\nfor block in \"$TSDB_PATH\"/*; do\n  if [[ -d \"$block\" && ! \"$block\" =~ wal$ ]]; then\n    if ! promtool tsdb inspect \"$block\" >/dev/null 2>&1; then\n      echo \"CORRUPTED: $block\"\n      mv \"$block\" \"$block.corrupted\"\n    fi\n  fi\ndone\n\n# 6. Restart\necho \"[6] Restarting Prometheus...\"\nsystemctl start prometheus\nsleep 5\n\n# 7. Verify\necho \"[7] Verification...\"\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy\necho \"\"\ntail -20 /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n```\n\n### Using promtool for Inspection & Recovery\n\n```bash\n# List all blocks with human-readable output\npromtool tsdb list /var/lib/prometheus --human-readable\n\n# Analyze compaction efficiency\npromtool tsdb analyze /var/lib/prometheus\n\n# Dump specific time range (for audit)\npromtool tsdb dump /var/lib/prometheus \\\n  --min-time=1609459200000 \\\n  --max-time=1609545600000 \\\n  --match='{job=\"prometheus\"}' > dump.txt\n\n# Verify block integrity\npromtool tsdb inspect /var/lib/prometheus/<ULID>\n\n# (Attempted) Repair corrupted blocks\npromtool tsdb repair /var/lib/prometheus\n```\n\n### Preventing Future Compaction Issues\n\n**Monitoring & Alerting:**\n\n```yaml\n# Prometheus alert rule example\ngroups:\n  - name: tsdb_compaction\n    rules:\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionsFailing\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[1h]) > 0\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compactions failing\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionStuck\n        expr: prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n          and changes(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[10m]) == 0\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compaction stuck for 10+ minutes\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBDiskSpaceRunningOut\n        expr: (prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes) > 0.85\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus disk usage > 85% of retention limit\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBCompactionTakingTooLong\n        expr: histogram_quantile(0.99, prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds) > 7200\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus p99 compaction duration > 2 hours (block range)\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusTSDBBlocksHighCardinality\n        expr: rate(prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total[5m]) > 0.1\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"High rate of vertical (overlapping) compactions\"\n```\n\n**Operational Best Practices:**\n\n1. **Retention Configuration**\n   - Size: Set `storage.tsdb.retention.size` to 80% of available disk\n   - Time: Balance query SLA (query_max_time) with storage costs\n   - Example: `retention.time=30d retention.size=500GB`\n\n2. **Resource Allocation**\n   - Memory: Allocate 2-4GB minimum; large cardinality may need 8-16GB\n   - CPU: Dedicate 2-4 cores to Prometheus; compaction uses all available\n   - Disk: Use SSDs; HDD I/O is major bottleneck\n\n3. **Cardinality Management**\n   - Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes`\n   - Use relabeling to drop high-cardinality labels\n   - Example: drop `pod_id`, `container_id` if not needed\n\n4. **High Availability**\n   - Run multiple Prometheus instances with remote storage\n   - Use WAL in remote storage for durability\n   - Federation for aggregation without compaction contention\n\n5. **Scheduled Maintenance**\n   - Weekly: `promtool tsdb analyze` for efficiency report\n   - Monthly: verify block checksums, backup critical blocks\n   - Quarterly: review retention policy based on query patterns\n\n---\n\n## 5. Code Reference: Key Functions\n\n### Compaction Triggering & Execution\n\n| Function | Location | Purpose |\n|----------|----------|---------|\n| `db.run()` | tsdb/db.go:982-1027 | Main compaction trigger event (line 1009) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | tsdb/db.go:297 | Counter | On compaction error (line 1140) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | tsdb/compact.go:107 | Gauge | Set 1 at line 748, 0 at line 746 |\n\n---\n\n## Appendix: Quick Reference\n\n### Command Cheat Sheet\n\n```bash\n# Check TSDB health\npromtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus --human-readable\n\n# Analyze blocks\npromtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus\n\n# Inspect specific block\npromtool tsdb inspect /path/to/prometheus/<ULID>\n\n# Dump samples for verification\npromtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus --min-time=<ts> --max-time=<ts>\n\n# Repair (use with caution)\npromtool tsdb repair /path/to/prometheus\n\n# Flush WAL to blocks (read-only scrape_interval: 15s\n\nstorage:\n  tsdb:\n    path: /var/lib/prometheus\n    retention:\n      time: 30d                          # Keep data 30 days\n      size: 500GB                        # OR max 500GB (whichever first)\n    max_block_chunk_segment_size: 536870912  # 512MB (default)\n\n# Command-line equivalent\n# --storage.tsdb.path=/var/lib/prometheus\n# --storage.tsdb.retention.time=30d\n# --storage.tsdb.retention.size=500GB\n# --storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size=536870912\n```\n\n### Sample Metric Queries\n\n```promql\n# Compaction prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds)\n\n# Block count\nprometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded\n\n# Storage usage\nprometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / 1e9  # In GB\n\n# Memory usage\nprocess_resident_memory_bytes / 1e9  # In GB\n\n# Disk saturation\nprometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nTSDB compaction is a critical background process for maintaining query performance and disk space efficiency. The key to operational stability is:\n\n1. **Monitor** compaction metrics continuously (failure count, duration, block count)\n2. **Alert** on anomalies (stuck compactions, failures, disk saturation)\n3. **Size** resources appropriately (memory, disk, CPU)\n4. **Plan** retention carefully (balance query window vs. storage cost)\n5. **Act quickly** when issues arise (recovery procedures in this runbook)\n\nMost issues can be prevented through proper sizing and monitoring. When incidents do occur, this runbook provides diagnostic procedures and recovery steps for rapid resolution.\n",

# Prometheus TSDB Compaction Operational Runbook

## 1. Overview

### What is Compaction?

TSDB compaction is the process of merging multiple time-series blocks into larger, more efficient blocks. It serves three primary purposes:

1. **Space Efficiency**: Consolidates data from smaller 2-hour blocks into larger blocks (up to 31 days or 10% of retention), reducing metadata overhead
2. **Query Performance**: Fewer blocks to scan during queries, reducing I/O and improving query speed
3. **Tombstone Cleanup**: Removes series marked for deletion (via tombstones), recovering disk space

### Block Structure

Prometheus stores time-series data in a hierarchical block structure with exponential block durations:

- **Level 0 (Head Block)**: In-memory head block, ~2 hours of data
- **Level 1-10**: Persisted blocks with exponentially increasing durations
  - Each level is ~3x larger than the previous level
  - Example: 2h → 6h → 18h → 54h → ... → 31 days
  - Blocks containing tombstones (>5% deleted series) are also compacted

### When Compaction is Triggered

Compaction is triggered through two mechanisms:

| Trigger Type | Frequency | Condition |
|---|---|---|
| **Head Block Compaction** | On append commit | `head.compactable()` returns true when head block age > `chunkRange / 2` |
| **Scheduled Compaction** | Every 1 minute | Regular background loop in `db.run()` checks for blocks ready to compact |
| **Block Compaction** | On-demand | Multiple level-0/1 blocks fitting within a time range are merged upward |

**Code References:**
- Head compaction trigger: `dbAppender.Commit()` (tsdb/db.go:1115-1127)
- Scheduled trigger: `db.run()` (tsdb/db.go:982-1027)
- Compaction logic: `db.Compact()` (tsdb/db.go:1133-1212)
